## <a name="locked-deployment-files"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-812">Arquivos de implantação bloqueados</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-812">Locked deployment files</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-813">Os arquivos na pasta de implantação são bloqueados quando o aplicativo está em execução.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-813">Files in the deployment folder are locked when the app is running.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-814">Os arquivos bloqueados não podem ser substituídos durante a implantação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-814">Locked files can't be overwritten during deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-815">Para liberar os arquivos bloqueados em uma implantação, interrompa o pool de aplicativos usando **uma** das abordagens a seguir:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-815">To release locked files in a deployment, stop the app pool using **one** of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-816">Use a Implantação da Web e referencie `Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web` no arquivo do projeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-816">Use Web Deploy and reference `Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web` in the project file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-817">Um arquivo *app_offline.htm* é colocado na raiz do diretório de aplicativo da Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-817">An *app_offline.htm* file is placed at the root of the web app directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-818">Quando o arquivo estiver presente, o módulo do ASP.NET Core apenas desligará o aplicativo e servirá o arquivo *app_offline.htm* durante a implantação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-818">When the file is present, the ASP.NET Core Module gracefully shuts down the app and serves the *app_offline.htm* file during the deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-819">Para obter mais informações, consulte [Referência de configuração do módulo do ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#app_offlinehtm).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-819">For more information, see the [ASP.NET Core Module configuration reference](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#app_offlinehtm).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-820">Manualmente interrompa o pool de aplicativos no Gerenciador do IIS no servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-820">Manually stop the app pool in the IIS Manager on the server.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-821">Use o PowerShell para descartar *App_offline. htm* (requer o PowerShell 5 ou posterior):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-821">Use PowerShell to drop *app_offline.htm* (requires PowerShell 5 or later):</span></span>

  ```powershell
  $pathToApp = 'PATH_TO_APP'

  # Stop the AppPool
  New-Item -Path $pathToApp app_offline.htm

  # Provide script commands here to deploy the app

  # Restart the AppPool
  Remove-Item -Path $pathToApp app_offline.htm

  ```

## <a name="data-protection"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-822">Proteção de dados</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-822">Data protection</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-823">A [pilha Proteção de Dados do ASP.NET Core](xref:security/data-protection/introduction) é usada por vários [middlewares](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) ASP.NET Core, incluindo aqueles usados na autenticação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-823">The [ASP.NET Core Data Protection stack](xref:security/data-protection/introduction) is used by several ASP.NET Core [middlewares](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index), including middleware used in authentication.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-824">Mesmo se as APIs de proteção de dados não forem chamadas pelo código do usuário, a proteção de dados deverá ser configurada com um script de implantação ou no código do usuário para criar um [repositório de chaves](xref:security/data-protection/implementation/key-management) criptográfico persistente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-824">Even if Data Protection APIs aren't called by user code, data protection should be configured with a deployment script or in user code to create a persistent cryptographic [key store](xref:security/data-protection/implementation/key-management).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-825">Se a proteção de dados não estiver configurada, as chaves serão mantidas na memória e descartadas quando o aplicativo for reiniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-825">If data protection isn't configured, the keys are held in memory and discarded when the app restarts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-826">Se o token de autenticação for armazenado na memória quando o aplicativo for reiniciado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-826">If the key ring is stored in memory when the app restarts:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-827">Todos os tokens de autenticação baseados em cookies serão invalidados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-827">All cookie-based authentication tokens are invalidated.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-828">Os usuários precisam entrar novamente na próxima solicitação deles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-828">Users are required to sign in again on their next request.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-829">Todos os dados protegidos com o token de autenticação não poderão mais ser descriptografados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-829">Any data protected with the key ring can no longer be decrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-830">Isso pode incluir [tokens CSRF](xref:security/anti-request-forgery#aspnet-core-antiforgery-configuration) e [ASP.NET Core cookies TempData do MVC](xref:fundamentals/app-state#tempdata).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-830">This may include [CSRF tokens](xref:security/anti-request-forgery#aspnet-core-antiforgery-configuration) and [ASP.NET Core MVC TempData cookies](xref:fundamentals/app-state#tempdata).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-831">Para configurar a proteção de dados no IIS para persistir o token de autenticação, use **uma** das seguintes abordagens:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-831">To configure data protection under IIS to persist the key ring, use **one** of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-832">**Criar chaves de registro de proteção de dados**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-832">**Create Data Protection Registry Keys**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-833">As chaves de proteção de dados usadas pelos aplicativos ASP.NET Core são armazenadas no registro externo aos aplicativos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-833">Data protection keys used by ASP.NET Core apps are stored in the registry external to the apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-834">Para persistir as chaves de determinado aplicativo, crie uma chave de registro para o pool de aplicativos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-834">To persist the keys for a given app, create registry keys for the app pool.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-835">Para instalações autônomas do IIS não Web Farm, você pode usar o [script Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1 de Proteção de Dados do PowerShell](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/DataProtection/Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1) para cada pool de aplicativos usado com um aplicativo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-835">For standalone, non-webfarm IIS installations, the [Data Protection Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1 PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/DataProtection/Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1) can be used for each app pool used with an ASP.NET Core app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-836">Esse script cria uma chave de registro no registro HKLM que é acessível apenas para a conta do processo de trabalho do pool de aplicativos do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-836">This script creates a registry key in the HKLM registry that's accessible only to the worker process account of the app's app pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-837">As chaves são criptografadas em repouso usando a DPAPI com uma chave para todo o computador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-837">Keys are encrypted at rest using DPAPI with a machine-wide key.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-838">Em cenários de web farm, um aplicativo pode ser configurado para usar um caminho UNC para armazenar seu token de autenticação de proteção de dados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-838">In web farm scenarios, an app can be configured to use a UNC path to store its data protection key ring.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-839">Por padrão, as chaves de proteção de dados não são criptografadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-839">By default, the data protection keys aren't encrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-840">Garanta que as permissões de arquivo de o compartilhamento de rede sejam limitadas à conta do Windows na qual o aplicativo é executado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-840">Ensure that the file permissions for the network share are limited to the Windows account the app runs under.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-841">Um certificado X509 pode ser usado para proteger chaves em repouso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-841">An X509 certificate can be used to protect keys at rest.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-842">Considere um mecanismo para permitir aos usuários carregar certificados: coloque os certificados no repositório de certificados confiáveis do usuário e certifique-se de que eles estejam disponíveis em todos os computadores nos quais o aplicativo do usuário é executado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-842">Consider a mechanism to allow users to upload certificates: Place certificates into the user's trusted certificate store and ensure they're available on all machines where the user's app runs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-843">Veja [Configurar a proteção de dados do ASP.NET Core](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview) para obter detalhes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-843">See [Configure ASP.NET Core Data Protection](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview) for details.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-844">**Configurar o pool de aplicativos do IIS para carregar o perfil do usuário**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-844">**Configure the IIS Application Pool to load the user profile**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-845">Essa configuração está na seção **Modelo de processo** nas **Configurações avançadas** do pool de aplicativos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-845">This setting is in the **Process Model** section under the **Advanced Settings** for the app pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-846">Defina **carregar perfil** do usuário `True`como.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-846">Set **Load User Profile** to `True`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-847">Quando definido como `True`, as chaves são armazenadas no diretório do perfil do usuário e protegidas usando DPAPI com uma chave específica para a conta de usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-847">When set to `True`, keys are stored in the user profile directory and protected using DPAPI with a key specific to the user account.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-848">As chaves são persistidas para a pasta *%LOCALAPPDATA%/ASP.NET/DataProtection-Keys*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-848">Keys are persisted to the *%LOCALAPPDATA%/ASP.NET/DataProtection-Keys* folder.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-849">O [atributo setProfileEnvironment](/iis/configuration/system.applicationhost/applicationpools/add/processmodel#configuration) do pool de aplicativos também deve ser habilitado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-849">The app pool's [setProfileEnvironment attribute](/iis/configuration/system.applicationhost/applicationpools/add/processmodel#configuration) must also be enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-850">O valor padrão de `setProfileEnvironment` é `true`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-850">The default value of `setProfileEnvironment` is `true`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-851">Em alguns cenários (por exemplo, um SO Windows), `setProfileEnvironment` é definido como `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-851">In some scenarios (for example, Windows OS), `setProfileEnvironment` is set to `false`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-852">Se as chaves não estiverem armazenadas no diretório do perfil do usuário como esperado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-852">If keys aren't stored in the user profile directory as expected:</span></span>

  1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-853">navegue até a pasta *%windir%/system32/inetsrv/config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-853">Navigate to the *%windir%/system32/inetsrv/config* folder.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-854">Abra o arquivo *applicationHost.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-854">Open the *applicationHost.config* file.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-855">Localize o elemento `<system.applicationHost><applicationPools><applicationPoolDefaults><processModel>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-855">Locate the `<system.applicationHost><applicationPools><applicationPoolDefaults><processModel>` element.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-856">Confirme se o atributo `setProfileEnvironment` não está presente, que tem como padrão o valor `true`, ou defina explicitamente o valor do atributo como `true`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-856">Confirm that the `setProfileEnvironment` attribute isn't present, which defaults the value to `true`, or explicitly set the attribute's value to `true`.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-857">**Usar o sistema de arquivos como um repositório de tokens de autenticação**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-857">**Use the file system as a key ring store**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-858">Ajuste o código do aplicativo para [usar o sistema de arquivos como um repositório de tokens de autenticação](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-858">Adjust the app code to [use the file system as a key ring store](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-859">Use um certificado X509 para proteger o token de autenticação e verifique se ele é um certificado confiável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-859">Use an X509 certificate to protect the key ring and ensure the certificate is a trusted certificate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-860">Se o certificado for autoassinado, você deverá colocá-lo no repositório Raiz confiável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-860">If the certificate is self-signed, place the certificate in the Trusted Root store.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-861">Ao usar o IIS em uma web farm:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-861">When using IIS in a web farm:</span></span>

  * <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-862">Use um compartilhamento de arquivos que pode ser acessado por todos os computadores.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-862">Use a file share that all machines can access.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-863">Implante um certificado X509 em cada computador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-863">Deploy an X509 certificate to each machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-864">Configure a [proteção de dados no código](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-864">Configure [data protection in code](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-865">**Definir uma política para todo o computador para proteção de dados**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-865">**Set a machine-wide policy for data protection**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-866">O sistema de proteção de dados tem suporte limitado para a configuração da [política de todo o computador](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/machine-wide-policy) padrão para todos os aplicativos que consomem as APIs de proteção de dados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-866">The data protection system has limited support for setting a default [machine-wide policy](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/machine-wide-policy) for all apps that consume the Data Protection APIs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-867">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:security/data-protection/introduction>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-867">For more information, see <xref:security/data-protection/introduction>.</span></span>

## <a name="virtual-directories"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-868">Diretórios virtuais</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-868">Virtual Directories</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-869">[Diretórios virtuais IIS](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#virtual-directories) não são compatíveis com aplicativos ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-869">[IIS Virtual Directories](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#virtual-directories) aren't supported with ASP.NET Core apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-870">Um aplicativo pode ser hospedado como um [subaplicativo](#sub-applications).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-870">An app can be hosted as a [sub-application](#sub-applications).</span></span>

## <a name="sub-applications"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-871">Subaplicativos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-871">Sub-applications</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-872">Um aplicativo ASP.NET Core pode ser hospedado como um [subaplicativo IIS (sub-app)](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#applications).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-872">An ASP.NET Core app can be hosted as an [IIS sub-application (sub-app)](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#applications).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-873">A parte do caminho do subaplicativo se torna parte da URL raiz do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-873">The sub-app's path becomes part of the root app's URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-874">Links de ativos estáticos dentro do subaplicativo devem usar a notação de sinal de til e barra (`~/`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-874">Static asset links within the sub-app should use tilde-slash (`~/`) notation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-875">A notação de sinal de til e barra aciona um [Auxiliar de Marca](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro) para preceder a base de caminho do subaplicativo ao link relativo renderizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-875">Tilde-slash notation triggers a [Tag Helper](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro) to prepend the sub-app's pathbase to the rendered relative link.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-876">Para um subaplicativo no `/subapp_path`, uma imagem vinculada com `src="~/image.png"` é renderizada como `src="/subapp_path/image.png"`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-876">For a sub-app at `/subapp_path`, an image linked with `src="~/image.png"` is rendered as `src="/subapp_path/image.png"`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-877">O Middleware de Arquivo Estático do aplicativo raiz não processa a solicitação de arquivo estático.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-877">The root app's Static File Middleware doesn't process the static file request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-878">A solicitação é processada pelo Middleware de Arquivo Estático do subaplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-878">The request is processed by the sub-app's Static File Middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-879">Se um atributo de ativo estático `src` for definido como um caminho absoluto (por exemplo, `src="/image.png"`), o link será renderizado sem a base de caminho do subaplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-879">If a static asset's `src` attribute is set to an absolute path (for example, `src="/image.png"`), the link is rendered without the sub-app's pathbase.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-880">O Middleware de Arquivos Estáticos do aplicativo raiz tenta fornecer o ativo do [webroot](xref:fundamentals/index#web-root) da raiz do aplicativo, que resulta em uma resposta *404 – Não encontrado*, a menos que o ativo estático esteja disponível no aplicativo raiz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-880">The root app's Static File Middleware attempts to serve the asset from the root app's [web root](xref:fundamentals/index#web-root), which results in a *404 - Not Found* response unless the static asset is available from the root app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-881">Para hospedar um aplicativo ASP.NET Core como um subaplicativo em outro aplicativo do ASP.NET Core:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-881">To host an ASP.NET Core app as a sub-app under another ASP.NET Core app:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-882">Estabeleça um pool de aplicativos para o subaplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-882">Establish an app pool for the sub-app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-883">Defina a **versão do CLR do .NET** como **Sem Código Gerenciado** porque o Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) do .NET Core é inicializado para hospedar o aplicativo no processo de trabalho, não no CLR de Área de trabalho (CLR do .NET).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-883">Set the **.NET CLR Version** to **No Managed Code** because the Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) for .NET Core is booted to host the app in the worker process, not the desktop CLR (.NET CLR).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-884">Adicione o site raiz no Gerenciador do IIS com o subaplicativo em uma pasta no site raiz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-884">Add the root site in IIS Manager with the sub-app in a folder under the root site.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-885">Clique com o botão direito do mouse na pasta do subaplicativo no Gerenciador do IIS e selecione **Converter em aplicativo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-885">Right-click the sub-app folder in IIS Manager and select **Convert to Application**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-886">Na caixa de diálogo **Adicionar Aplicativo**, use o botão **Selecionar** no **Pool de Aplicativos** para atribuir o pool de aplicativos que você criou ao subaplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-886">In the **Add Application** dialog, use the **Select** button for the **Application Pool** to assign the app pool that you created for the sub-app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-887">Selecione **OK**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-887">Select **OK**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-888">A atribuição de um pool de aplicativos separado para o subaplicativo é um requisito ao usar o modelo de hospedagem em processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-888">The assignment of a separate app pool to the sub-app is a requirement when using the in-process hosting model.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-889">Para obter mais informações sobre o modelo de hospedagem em processo e como configurar o módulo ASP.NET Core <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>, consulte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-889">For more information on the in-process hosting model and configuring the ASP.NET Core Module, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

## <a name="configuration-of-iis-with-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-890">Configuração do IIS com web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-890">Configuration of IIS with web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-891">A configuração do IIS é influenciada pela seção `<system.webServer>` do *web.config* para cenários do IIS que são funcionais para aplicativos ASP.NET Core com o Módulo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-891">IIS configuration is influenced by the `<system.webServer>` section of *web.config* for IIS scenarios that are functional for ASP.NET Core apps with the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-892">Por exemplo, a configuração do IIS é funcional para a compactação dinâmica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-892">For example, IIS configuration is functional for dynamic compression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-893">Se o IIS for configurado no nível do servidor para usar a compactação dinâmica, o elemento `<urlCompression>` no arquivo *web.config* do aplicativo pode desabilitá-la para um aplicativo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-893">If IIS is configured at the server level to use dynamic compression, the `<urlCompression>` element in the app's *web.config* file can disable it for an ASP.NET Core app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-894">Para obter mais informações, consulte estes tópicos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-894">For more information, see the following topics:</span></span>

* [<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-895">Referência de configuração \<para System. webserver></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-895">Configuration reference for \<system.webServer></span></span>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/)
* <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>
* <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-896">Para definir variáveis de ambiente para aplicativos individuais executados em pools de aplicativos isolados (compatível com o IIS 10.0+ ou posterior), veja a seção *comando AppCmd.exe* do tópico [Variáveis de ambiente \<environmentVariables>](/iis/configuration/system.applicationHost/applicationPools/add/environmentVariables/#appcmdexe) na documentação de referência do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-896">To set environment variables for individual apps running in isolated app pools (supported for IIS 10.0 or later), see the *AppCmd.exe command* section of the [Environment Variables \<environmentVariables>](/iis/configuration/system.applicationHost/applicationPools/add/environmentVariables/#appcmdexe) topic in the IIS reference documentation.</span></span>

## <a name="configuration-sections-of-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-897">Seções de configuração de web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-897">Configuration sections of web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-898">As seções de configuração de aplicativos ASP.NET 4.x em *web.config* não são usadas por aplicativos ASP.NET Core para configuração:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-898">Configuration sections of ASP.NET 4.x apps in *web.config* aren't used by ASP.NET Core apps for configuration:</span></span>

* `<system.web>`
* `<appSettings>`
* `<connectionStrings>`
* `<location>`

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-899">Aplicativos ASP.NET Core são configurados para usar outros provedores de configuração.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-899">ASP.NET Core apps are configured using other configuration providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-900">Para obter mais informações, consulte [Configuration](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-900">For more information, see [Configuration](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index).</span></span>

## <a name="application-pools"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-901">Pools de aplicativos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-901">Application Pools</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-902">O isolamento do pool de aplicativos é determinado pelo modelo de hospedagem:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-902">App pool isolation is determined by the hosting model:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-903">Hospedagem em processo &ndash; Aplicativos são necessários para execução em pools de aplicativos separados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-903">In-process hosting &ndash; Apps are required to run in separate app pools.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-904">Hospedagem fora do processo &ndash; É recomendável isolar os aplicativos uns dos outros, executando cada aplicativo em seu próprio pool de aplicativos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-904">Out-of-process hosting &ndash; We recommend isolating the apps from each other by running each app in its own app pool.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-905">A caixa de diálogo **Adicionar Site** do IIS usa como padrão um único pool de aplicativos por aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-905">The IIS **Add Website** dialog defaults to a single app pool per app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-906">Quando um **Nome de site** é fornecido, o texto é transferido automaticamente para a caixa de texto **Pool de aplicativos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-906">When a **Site name** is provided, the text is automatically transferred to the **Application pool** textbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-907">Um novo pool de aplicativos é criado usando o nome do site quando você adicionar o site.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-907">A new app pool is created using the site name when the site is added.</span></span>

## <a name="application-pool-identity"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-908">Identidade do pool de aplicativos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-908">Application Pool Identity</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-909">Uma conta de identidade do pool de aplicativos permite executar um aplicativo em uma conta exclusiva sem a necessidade de criar e gerenciar domínios ou contas locais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-909">An app pool identity account allows an app to run under a unique account without having to create and manage domains or local accounts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-910">No IIS 8.0 ou posterior, o WAS (Processo de trabalho do administrador) do IIS cria uma conta virtual com o nome do novo pool de aplicativos e executa os processos de trabalho do pool de aplicativos nesta conta por padrão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-910">On IIS 8.0 or later, the IIS Admin Worker Process (WAS) creates a virtual account with the name of the new app pool and runs the app pool's worker processes under this account by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-911">No Console de Gerenciamento do IIS, em **Configurações avançadas** do pool de aplicativos, verifique se a **Identidade** é definida para usar **ApplicationPoolIdentity**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-911">In the IIS Management Console under **Advanced Settings** for the app pool, ensure that the **Identity** is set to use **ApplicationPoolIdentity**:</span></span>

![Caixa de diálogo Configurações avançadas do pool de aplicativos](index/_static/apppool-identity.png)

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-913">O processo de gerenciamento do IIS cria um identificador seguro com o nome do pool de aplicativos no Sistema de segurança do Windows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-913">The IIS management process creates a secure identifier with the name of the app pool in the Windows Security System.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-914">Os recursos podem ser protegidos usando essa identidade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-914">Resources can be secured using this identity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-915">No entanto, essa identidade não é uma conta de usuário real e não será mostrada no Console de Gerenciamento de Usuários do Windows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-915">However, this identity isn't a real user account and doesn't show up in the Windows User Management Console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-916">Se o processo de trabalho do IIS requerer acesso elevado ao aplicativo, modifique a ACL (lista de controle de acesso) do diretório que contém o aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-916">If the IIS worker process requires elevated access to the app, modify the Access Control List (ACL) for the directory containing the app:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-917">Abra o Windows Explorer e navegue para o diretório.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-917">Open Windows Explorer and navigate to the directory.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-918">Clique com o botão direito do mouse no diretório e selecione **Propriedades**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-918">Right-click on the directory and select **Properties**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-919">Na guia **Segurança**, selecione o botão **Editar** e, em seguida, no botão **Adicionar**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-919">Under the **Security** tab, select the **Edit** button and then the **Add** button.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-920">Clique no botão **Locais** e verifique se o sistema está selecionado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-920">Select the **Locations** button and make sure the system is selected.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-921">Insira **IIS AppPool\\<nome_pool_aplicativos>** na área **Inserir os nomes de objeto a serem selecionados**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-921">Enter **IIS AppPool\\<app_pool_name>** in **Enter the object names to select** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-922">Selecione o botão **Verificar Nomes**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-922">Select the **Check Names** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-923">Para o *DefaultAppPool*, verifique os nomes usando **IIS AppPool\DefaultAppPool**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-923">For the *DefaultAppPool* check the names using **IIS AppPool\DefaultAppPool**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-924">Quando o botão **Verificar Nomes** é selecionado, um valor de **DefaultAppPool** é indicado na área de nomes de objeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-924">When the **Check Names** button is selected, a value of **DefaultAppPool** is indicated in the object names area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-925">Não é possível inserir o nome do pool de aplicativos diretamente na área de nomes de objeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-925">It isn't possible to enter the app pool name directly into the object names area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-926">Use o formato **IIS AppPool\\<nome_pool_aplicativos>** ao verificar o nome do objeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-926">Use the **IIS AppPool\\<app_pool_name>** format when checking for the object name.</span></span>

   ![Selecione a caixa de diálogo de usuários ou grupos para a pasta do aplicativo: o nome do pool de aplicativos "DefaultAppPool" é anexado ao "IIS AppPool\" na área de nomes de objeto antes de selecionar"Verificar Nomes".](index/_static/select-users-or-groups-1.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-928">Selecione **OK**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-928">Select **OK**.</span></span>

   ![Selecione a caixa de diálogo de usuários ou grupos para a pasta do aplicativo: depois de selecionar "Verificar Nomes", o nome do objeto "DefaultAppPool" é mostrado na área de nomes de objeto.](index/_static/select-users-or-groups-2.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-930">As permissões de leitura &amp; execução devem ser concedidas por padrão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-930">Read &amp; execute permissions should be granted by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-931">Forneça permissões adicionais conforme necessário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-931">Provide additional permissions as needed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-932">O acesso também pode ser concedido por meio de um prompt de comando usando a ferramenta **ICACLS**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-932">Access can also be granted at a command prompt using the **ICACLS** tool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-933">Usando o *DefaultAppPool* como exemplo, o comando a seguir é usado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-933">Using the *DefaultAppPool* as an example, the following command is used:</span></span>

```console
ICACLS C:\sites\MyWebApp /grant "IIS AppPool\DefaultAppPool":F
```

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-934">Para saber mais, veja o tópico [icacls](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/icacls).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-934">For more information, see the [icacls](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/icacls) topic.</span></span>

## <a name="http2-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-935">Suporte do HTTP/2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-935">HTTP/2 support</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-936">O [HTTP/2](https://httpwg.org/specs/rfc7540.html) é compatível com ASP.NET Core nos seguintes cenários de implantação de IIS:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-936">[HTTP/2](https://httpwg.org/specs/rfc7540.html) is supported with ASP.NET Core in the following IIS deployment scenarios:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-937">Em processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-937">In-process</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-938">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 ou posterior; IIS 10 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-938">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 or later; IIS 10 or later</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-939">Conexão TLS 1.2 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-939">TLS 1.2 or later connection</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-940">Fora do processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-940">Out-of-process</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-941">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 ou posterior; IIS 10 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-941">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 or later; IIS 10 or later</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-942">Conexões de servidor de borda voltadas para o público usam HTTP/2, mas a conexão de proxy reverso para o [servidor Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) usa HTTP/1.1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-942">Public-facing edge server connections use HTTP/2, but the reverse proxy connection to the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) uses HTTP/1.1.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-943">Conexão TLS 1.2 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-943">TLS 1.2 or later connection</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-944">Para uma implantação em processo quando uma conexão HTTP/2 for estabelecida, o [HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) relatará `HTTP/2`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-944">For an in-process deployment when an HTTP/2 connection is established, [HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) reports `HTTP/2`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-945">Para uma implantação fora de processo quando uma conexão HTTP/2 for estabelecida, o [HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) relatará `HTTP/1.1`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-945">For an out-of-process deployment when an HTTP/2 connection is established, [HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) reports `HTTP/1.1`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-946">Para saber mais sobre os modelos de hospedagem em processo e fora de processo, confira <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-946">For more information on the in-process and out-of-process hosting models, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-947">O HTTP/2 está habilitado por padrão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-947">HTTP/2 is enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-948">As conexões retornarão para HTTP/1.1 se uma conexão HTTP/2 não for estabelecida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-948">Connections fall back to HTTP/1.1 if an HTTP/2 connection isn't established.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-949">Para obter mais informações sobre a configuração de HTTP/2 com implantações do IIS, consulte [HTTP/2 no IIS](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-10/http2-on-iis).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-949">For more information on HTTP/2 configuration with IIS deployments, see [HTTP/2 on IIS](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-10/http2-on-iis).</span></span>

## <a name="cors-preflight-requests"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-950">Solicitações de simulação do CORS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-950">CORS preflight requests</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-951">*Esta seção só se aplica a aplicativos ASP.NET Core com o .NET Framework como destino.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-951">*This section only applies to ASP.NET Core apps that target the .NET Framework.*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-952">Para um aplicativo ASP.NET Core com o .NET Framework como destino, as solicitações OPTIONS não são passadas para o aplicativo por padrão no IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-952">For an ASP.NET Core app that targets the .NET Framework, OPTIONS requests aren't passed to the app by default in IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-953">Para saber como configurar os manipuladores do IIS do aplicativo no *Web. config* para passar solicitações de opções, consulte [habilitar solicitações entre origens no ASP.NET Web API 2: como o CORS funciona](/aspnet/web-api/overview/security/enabling-cross-origin-requests-in-web-api#how-cors-works).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-953">To learn how to configure the app's IIS handlers in *web.config* to pass OPTIONS requests, see [Enable cross-origin requests in ASP.NET Web API 2: How CORS Works](/aspnet/web-api/overview/security/enabling-cross-origin-requests-in-web-api#how-cors-works).</span></span>

## <a name="application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-954">Módulo de Inicialização de Aplicativo e Tempo Limite de Ociosidade</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-954">Application Initialization Module and Idle Timeout</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-955">Quando hospedado no IIS pela versão 2 do Módulo do ASP.NET Core:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-955">When hosted in IIS by the ASP.NET Core Module version 2:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-956">O [aplicativo do módulo](#application-initialization-module) &ndash; de inicialização [de aplicativos hospedado em processo](#in-process-hosting-model) ou [fora do processo](#out-of-process-hosting-model) pode ser configurado para iniciar automaticamente em uma reinicialização do processo de trabalho ou reinicialização do servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-956">[Application Initialization Module](#application-initialization-module) &ndash; App's hosted [in-process](#in-process-hosting-model) or [out-of-process](#out-of-process-hosting-model) can be configured to start automatically on a worker process restart or server restart.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-957">[Tempo Limite de Ociosidade](#idle-timeout) &ndash; Aplicativos hospedados [em processo](#in-process-hosting-model) podem ser configurados para não atingir o tempo limite durante períodos de inatividade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-957">[Idle Timeout](#idle-timeout) &ndash; App's hosted [in-process](#in-process-hosting-model) can be configured not to timeout during periods of inactivity.</span></span>

### <a name="application-initialization-module"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-958">Módulo de Inicialização de Aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-958">Application Initialization Module</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-959">*Aplica-se a aplicativos hospedados em processo e fora de processo.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-959">*Applies to apps hosted in-process and out-of-process.*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-960">[Inicialização de Aplicativo IIS](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-8/iis-80-application-initialization) é um recurso do IIS que envia uma solicitação HTTP para o aplicativo quando o pool de aplicativos é iniciado ou reciclado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-960">[IIS Application Initialization](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-8/iis-80-application-initialization) is an IIS feature that sends an HTTP request to the app when the app pool starts or is recycled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-961">A solicitação dispara a inicialização do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-961">The request triggers the app to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-962">Por padrão, o IIS emite uma solicitação para a URL raiz do aplicativo (`/`) para inicializar o aplicativo (confira mais detalhes sobre a configuração nos [recursos adicionais](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout-additional-resources)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-962">By default, IIS issues a request to the app's root URL (`/`) to initialize the app (see the [additional resources](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout-additional-resources) for more details on configuration).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-963">Confirme se o recurso da função Inicialização de Aplicativo do IIS está habilitado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-963">Confirm that the IIS Application Initialization role feature in enabled:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-964">No Windows 7 ou sistemas de área de trabalho posteriores, ao usar o IIS localmente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-964">On Windows 7 or later desktop systems when using IIS locally:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-965">Navegue até **Painel de Controle** > **Programas** > **Programas e Recursos** > **Ativar ou desativar recursos do Windows** (lado esquerdo da tela).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-965">Navigate to **Control Panel** > **Programs** > **Programs and Features** > **Turn Windows features on or off** (left side of the screen).</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-966">Abra **Serviços de Informações da Internet** > **Serviços da World Wide Web** > **Recursos de Desenvolvimento de Aplicativos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-966">Open **Internet Information Services** > **World Wide Web Services** > **Application Development Features**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-967">Marque a caixa de seleção **Inicialização de Aplicativo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-967">Select the check box for **Application Initialization**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-968">No Windows Server 2008 R2 ou posterior:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-968">On Windows Server 2008 R2 or later:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-969">Abra o **Assistente de Adição de Funções e Recursos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-969">Open the **Add Roles and Features Wizard**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-970">No painel **Selecionar serviços de função**, abra o nó **Desenvolvimento de aplicativos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-970">In the **Select role services** panel, open the **Application Development** node.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-971">Marque a caixa de seleção **Inicialização de Aplicativo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-971">Select the check box for **Application Initialization**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-972">Use quaisquer das abordagens a seguir para habilitar o Módulo de Inicialização do Aplicativo para o site:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-972">Use either of the following approaches to enable the Application Initialization Module for the site:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-973">Usando o Gerenciador do IIS:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-973">Using IIS Manager:</span></span>

  1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-974">Selecione **Pools de Aplicativos** no painel **Conexões**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-974">Select **Application Pools** in the **Connections** panel.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-975">Clique com o botão direito do mouse no pool de aplicativos do aplicativo na lista e selecione **Configurações Avançadas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-975">Right-click the app's app pool in the list and select **Advanced Settings**.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-976">O **Modo de Inicialização** padrão é **OnDemand**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-976">The default **Start Mode** is **OnDemand**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-977">Defina o **Modo de Inicialização** como **AlwaysRunning**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-977">Set the **Start Mode** to **AlwaysRunning**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-978">Selecione **OK**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-978">Select **OK**.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-979">Abra o nó **Sites** no painel **Conexões**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-979">Open the **Sites** node in the **Connections** panel.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-980">Clique com o botão direito do mouse no aplicativo e selecione **Gerenciar Site** > **Configurações Avançadas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-980">Right-click the app and select **Manage Website** > **Advanced Settings**.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-981">A configuração de **Pré-carregamento Habilitado** padrão é **Falso**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-981">The default **Preload Enabled** setting is **False**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-982">Defina **Pré-carregamento Habilitado** como **Verdadeiro**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-982">Set **Preload Enabled** to **True**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-983">Selecione **OK**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-983">Select **OK**.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-984">Usando o *web.config*, adicione o elemento `<applicationInitialization>` definindo `doAppInitAfterRestart` como `true` aos elementos `<system.webServer>` no arquivo *web.config* do aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-984">Using *web.config*, add the `<applicationInitialization>` element with `doAppInitAfterRestart` set to `true` to the `<system.webServer>` elements in the app's *web.config* file:</span></span>

  ```xml
  <?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
  <configuration>
    <location path="." inheritInChildApplications="false">
      <system.webServer>
        <applicationInitialization doAppInitAfterRestart="true" />
      </system.webServer>
    </location>
  </configuration>
  ```

### <a name="idle-timeout"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-985">Tempo limite de ociosidade</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-985">Idle Timeout</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-986">*Só se aplica a aplicativos hospedados em processo.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-986">*Only applies to apps hosted in-process.*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-987">Para impedir que o aplicativo fique ocioso, defina o tempo limite de ociosidade do pool de aplicativos, usando o Gerenciador do IIS:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-987">To prevent the app from idling, set the app pool's idle timeout using IIS Manager:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-988">Selecione **Pools de Aplicativos** no painel **Conexões**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-988">Select **Application Pools** in the **Connections** panel.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-989">Clique com o botão direito do mouse no pool de aplicativos do aplicativo na lista e selecione **Configurações Avançadas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-989">Right-click the app's app pool in the list and select **Advanced Settings**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-990">O **Tempo Limite de Ociosidade (minutos)** é de **20** minutos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-990">The default **Idle Time-out (minutes)** is **20** minutes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-991">Defina o **Tempo Limite de Ociosidade (minutos)** como **0** (zero).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-991">Set the **Idle Time-out (minutes)** to **0** (zero).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-992">Selecione **OK**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-992">Select **OK**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-993">Recicle o processo de trabalho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-993">Recycle the worker process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-994">Para impedir que aplicativos hospedados [fora de processo](#out-of-process-hosting-model) atinjam o tempo limite, use uma das seguintes abordagens:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-994">To prevent apps hosted [out-of-process](#out-of-process-hosting-model) from timing out, use either of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-995">Execute ping do aplicativo de um serviço externo para mantê-lo em execução.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-995">Ping the app from an external service in order to keep it running.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-996">Se o aplicativo hospedar apenas serviços em segundo plano, evite a hospedagem do IIS e use um [Serviço do Windows para hospedar o aplicativo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/windows-service).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-996">If the app only hosts background services, avoid IIS hosting and use a [Windows Service to host the ASP.NET Core app](xref:host-and-deploy/windows-service).</span></span>

### <a name="application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout-additional-resources"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-997">Recursos adicionais do Módulo de Inicialização de Aplicativo e do Tempo Limite de Ociosidade</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-997">Application Initialization Module and Idle Timeout additional resources</span></span>

## <a name="supported-operating-systems"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1011">Sistemas operacionais com suporte</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1011">Supported operating systems</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1012">Há suporte para os seguintes sistemas operacionais:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1012">The following operating systems are supported:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1013">Windows 7 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1013">Windows 7 or later</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1014">Windows Server 2008 R2 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1014">Windows Server 2008 R2 or later</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1015">O [servidor HTTP.sys](xref:fundamentals/servers/httpsys) (anteriormente chamado de WebListener) não funciona em uma configuração de proxy reverso com o IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1015">[HTTP.sys server](xref:fundamentals/servers/httpsys) (formerly called WebListener) doesn't work in a reverse proxy configuration with IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1016">Use o [servidor Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1016">Use the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1017">Para obter mais informações sobre hospedagem no Azure, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/azure-apps/index>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1017">For information on hosting in Azure, see <xref:host-and-deploy/azure-apps/index>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1018">Para obter as diretrizes de solução de problemas, consulte <xref:test/troubleshoot>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1018">For troubleshooting guidance, see <xref:test/troubleshoot>.</span></span>

## <a name="supported-platforms"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1019">Plataformas com suporte</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1019">Supported platforms</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1020">Aplicativos publicados para implantação de 32 bits (x86) ou 64 bits (x64) têm suporte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1020">Apps published for 32-bit (x86) or 64-bit (x64) deployment are supported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1021">Implantar um aplicativo de 32 bits com um SDK do .NET Core de 32 bits (x86), a menos que o aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1021">Deploy a 32-bit app with a 32-bit (x86) .NET Core SDK unless the app:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1022">Exija o maior espaço de endereço de memória virtual disponível para um aplicativo de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1022">Requires the larger virtual memory address space available to a 64-bit app.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1023">Exija o maior tamanho de pilha do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1023">Requires the larger IIS stack size.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1024">Tenha dependências nativas de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1024">Has 64-bit native dependencies.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1025">Use um SDK do .NET Core de 64 bits (x64) para publicar um aplicativo de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1025">Use a 64-bit (x64) .NET Core SDK to publish a 64-bit app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1026">Um runtime de 64 bits deve estar presente no sistema host.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1026">A 64-bit runtime must be present on the host system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1027">O ASP.NET Core vem com o [servidor Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel), um servidor HTTP padrão multiplataforma.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1027">ASP.NET Core ships with [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel), a default, cross-platform HTTP server.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1028">Ao usar o [IIS](/iis/get-started/introduction-to-iis/introduction-to-iis-architecture) ou o [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview), o aplicativo é executado em um processo separado do processo de trabalho do IIS (*fora do processo*) com o [servidor Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/index#kestrel).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1028">When using [IIS](/iis/get-started/introduction-to-iis/introduction-to-iis-architecture) or [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview), the app runs in a process separate from the IIS worker process (*out-of-process*) with the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/index#kestrel).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1029">Como os aplicativos ASP.NET Core são executados em um processo separado do processo de trabalho do IIS, o módulo realiza o gerenciamento de processos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1029">Because ASP.NET Core apps run in a process separate from the IIS worker process, the module handles process management.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1030">O módulo inicia o processo para o aplicativo ASP.NET Core quando a primeira solicitação chega e reinicia o aplicativo se ele é desligado ou falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1030">The module starts the process for the ASP.NET Core app when the first request arrives and restarts the app if it shuts down or crashes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1031">Isso é basicamente o mesmo comportamento que o dos aplicativos que são executados dentro do processo e são gerenciados pelo [WAS (Serviço de Ativação de Processos do Windows)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1031">This is essentially the same behavior as seen with apps that run in-process that are managed by the [Windows Process Activation Service (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1032">O diagrama a seguir ilustra a relação entre o IIS, o Módulo do ASP.NET Core e um aplicativo hospedado de fora d processo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1032">The following diagram illustrates the relationship between IIS, the ASP.NET Core Module, and an app hosted out-of-process:</span></span>

![Módulo do ASP.NET Core](index/_static/ancm-outofprocess.png)

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1034">As solicitações chegam da Web para o driver do HTTP.sys no modo kernel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1034">Requests arrive from the web to the kernel-mode HTTP.sys driver.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1035">O driver roteia as solicitações ao IIS na porta configurada do site, normalmente, a 80 (HTTP) ou a 443 (HTTPS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1035">The driver routes the requests to IIS on the website's configured port, usually 80 (HTTP) or 443 (HTTPS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1036">O módulo encaminha as solicitações ao Kestrel em uma porta aleatória do aplicativo, que não seja a porta 80 ou 443.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1036">The module forwards the requests to Kestrel on a random port for the app, which isn't port 80 or 443.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1037">O módulo Especifica a porta por meio de uma variável de ambiente na inicialização, e o [middleware de integração do IIS](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#enable-the-iisintegration-components) configura o servidor a `http://localhost:{port}`ser escutado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1037">The module specifies the port via an environment variable at startup, and the [IIS Integration Middleware](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#enable-the-iisintegration-components) configures the server to listen on `http://localhost:{port}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1038">Outras verificações são executadas e as solicitações que não se originam do módulo são rejeitadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1038">Additional checks are performed, and requests that don't originate from the module are rejected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1039">O módulo não é compatível com encaminhamento de HTTPS, portanto, as solicitações são encaminhadas por HTTP, mesmo se recebidas pelo IIS por HTTPS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1039">The module doesn't support HTTPS forwarding, so requests are forwarded over HTTP even if received by IIS over HTTPS.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1040">Depois que o Kestrel coleta a solicitação do módulo, a solicitação é enviada por push ao pipeline do middleware do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1040">After Kestrel picks up the request from the module, the request is pushed into the ASP.NET Core middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1041">O pipeline do middleware manipula a solicitação e a passa como uma instância de `HttpContext` para a lógica do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1041">The middleware pipeline handles the request and passes it on as an `HttpContext` instance to the app's logic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1042">O middleware adicionado pela integração do IIS atualiza o esquema, o IP remoto e pathbase para encaminhar a solicitação para o Kestrel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1042">Middleware added by IIS Integration updates the scheme, remote IP, and pathbase to account for forwarding the request to Kestrel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1043">A resposta do aplicativo é retornada ao IIS, que a retorna por push para o cliente HTTP que iniciou a solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1043">The app's response is passed back to IIS, which pushes it back out to the HTTP client that initiated the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1044">`CreateDefaultBuilder` configura o servidor [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) como o servidor Web e habilita a integração do IIS, configurando o caminho base e a porta para o [Módulo do ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1044">`CreateDefaultBuilder` configures [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) server as the web server and enables IIS Integration by configuring the base path and port for the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1045">O Módulo do ASP.NET Core gera uma porta dinâmica a ser atribuída ao processo de back-end.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1045">The ASP.NET Core Module generates a dynamic port to assign to the backend process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1046">`CreateDefaultBuilder` chama o método <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1046">`CreateDefaultBuilder` calls the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration*> method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1047">`UseIISIntegration` configura o Kestrel para escutar na porta dinâmica no endereço IP do localhost (`127.0.0.1`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1047">`UseIISIntegration` configures Kestrel to listen on the dynamic port at the localhost IP address (`127.0.0.1`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1048">Se a porta dinâmica for 1234, o Kestrel escutará em `127.0.0.1:1234`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1048">If the dynamic port is 1234, Kestrel listens at `127.0.0.1:1234`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1049">Essa configuração substitui outras configurações de URL fornecidas por:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1049">This configuration replaces other URL configurations provided by:</span></span>

* `UseUrls`
* [<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1050">API de escuta do Kestrel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1050">Kestrel's Listen API</span></span>](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel#endpoint-configuration)
* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1051">[Configuração](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index) (ou [opção --urls de linha de comando](xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#override-configuration))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1051">[Configuration](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index) (or [command-line --urls option](xref:fundamentals/host/web-host#override-configuration))</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1052">As chamadas a `UseUrls` ou à API `Listen` do Kestrel não são necessárias ao usar o módulo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1052">Calls to `UseUrls` or Kestrel's `Listen` API aren't required when using the module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1053">Se `UseUrls` ou `Listen` for chamado, o Kestrel escutará na porta especificada somente durante a execução do aplicativo sem o IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1053">If `UseUrls` or `Listen` is called, Kestrel listens on the port specified only when running the app without IIS.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1054">Para orientação sobre a configuração do Módulo do ASP.NET Core, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1054">For ASP.NET Core Module configuration guidance, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1055">Para saber mais sobre hospedagem, confira [Host no ASP.NET Core](xref:fundamentals/index#host).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1055">For more information on hosting, see [Host in ASP.NET Core](xref:fundamentals/index#host).</span></span>

## <a name="application-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1056">Configuração de aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1056">Application configuration</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-iisintegration-components"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1057">Habilitar os componentes de IISIntegration</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1057">Enable the IISIntegration components</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1058">Ao criar um host no `CreateWebHostBuilder` (*Program.cs*), chame <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.WebHost.CreateDefaultBuilder*> para habilitar a integração do IIS:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1058">When building a host in `CreateWebHostBuilder` (*Program.cs*), call <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.WebHost.CreateDefaultBuilder*> to enable IIS integration:</span></span>

```csharp
public static IWebHostBuilder CreateWebHostBuilder(string[] args) =>
    WebHost.CreateDefaultBuilder(args)
        ...
```
