## <a name="install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1146">Instalar o pacote de hospedagem do .NET Core</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1146">Install the .NET Core Hosting Bundle</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1147">Instale o *pacote de hospedagem do .NET Core* no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1147">Install the *.NET Core Hosting Bundle* on the hosting system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1148">O pacote instala o tempo de execução do .NET Core, a biblioteca do .NET Core e o [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1148">The bundle installs the .NET Core Runtime, .NET Core Library, and the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1149">O módulo permite que aplicativos do ASP.NET Core sejam executados por trás do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1149">The module allows ASP.NET Core apps to run behind IIS.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1150">Se o pacote de hospedagem for instalado antes do IIS, a instalação do pacote deverá ser reparada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1150">If the Hosting Bundle is installed before IIS, the bundle installation must be repaired.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1151">Execute o instalador do pacote de hospedagem novamente depois de instalar o IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1151">Run the Hosting Bundle installer again after installing IIS.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1152">Se o pacote de hospedagem for instalado após a instalação da versão de 64 bits (x64) do .NET Core, os SDKs poderão parecer estar ausentes ([Nenhum SDK do .NET Core foi detectado](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1152">If the Hosting Bundle is installed after installing the 64-bit (x64) version of .NET Core, SDKs might appear to be missing ([No .NET Core SDKs were detected](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1153">Para resolver o problema, consulte <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1153">To resolve the problem, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>.</span></span>

### <a name="download"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1154">Baixar</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1154">Download</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1155">Navegue até a página [baixar o .NET Core](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/download/dotnet-core) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1155">Navigate to the [Download .NET Core](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/download/dotnet-core) page.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1156">Selecione a versão do .NET Core desejada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1156">Select the desired .NET Core version.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1157">Na coluna **Executar aplicativos – runtime**, localize a linha da versão de runtime do .NET Core desejada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1157">In the **Run apps - Runtime** column, find the row of the .NET Core runtime version desired.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1158">Baixe o instalador usando o link **pacote de hospedagem** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1158">Download the installer using the **Hosting Bundle** link.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1159">Alguns instaladores contêm versões de lançamento que atingiram o EOL (fim da vida útil) e não têm mais suporte da Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1159">Some installers contain release versions that have reached their end of life (EOL) and are no longer supported by Microsoft.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1160">Para saber mais, confira a [política de suporte](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/platform/support/policy/dotnet-core).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1160">For more information, see the [support policy](https://dotnet.microsoft.com/platform/support/policy/dotnet-core).</span></span>

### <a name="install-the-hosting-bundle"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1161">Instalar o pacote de hospedagem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1161">Install the Hosting Bundle</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1162">Execute o instalador no servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1162">Run the installer on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1163">Os parâmetros a seguir estão disponíveis ao executar o instalador por meio de um shell de comando do administrador:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1163">The following parameters are available when running the installer from an administrator command shell:</span></span>

   * <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1164">`OPT_NO_ANCM=1`&ndash; Ignorar a instalação do módulo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1164">`OPT_NO_ANCM=1` &ndash; Skip installing the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1165">`OPT_NO_RUNTIME=1`&ndash; Ignorar a instalação do tempo de execução do .NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1165">`OPT_NO_RUNTIME=1` &ndash; Skip installing the .NET Core runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1166">Usado quando o servidor hospeda apenas [implantações independentes (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1166">Used when the server only hosts [self-contained deployments (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1167">`OPT_NO_SHAREDFX=1`&ndash; Ignorar a instalação da estrutura compartilhada ASP.NET (ASP.net Runtime).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1167">`OPT_NO_SHAREDFX=1` &ndash; Skip installing the ASP.NET Shared Framework (ASP.NET runtime).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1168">Usado quando o servidor hospeda apenas [implantações independentes (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1168">Used when the server only hosts [self-contained deployments (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1169">`OPT_NO_X86=1`&ndash; Ignorar a instalação de tempos de execução x86.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1169">`OPT_NO_X86=1` &ndash; Skip installing x86 runtimes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1170">Use esse parâmetro quando você souber que não hospedará aplicativos de 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1170">Use this parameter when you know that you won't be hosting 32-bit apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1171">Se houver uma possibilidade de hospedar aplicativos de 32 bits e 64 bits no futuro, não use esse parâmetro e instale ambos os runtimes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1171">If there's any chance that you will host both 32-bit and 64-bit apps in the future, don't use this parameter and install both runtimes.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1172">`OPT_NO_SHARED_CONFIG_CHECK=1` &ndash; Desabilite a verificação para usar uma Configuração Compartilhada do IIS quando a configuração compartilhada (*applicationHost.config*) estiver no mesmo computador do que a instalação do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1172">`OPT_NO_SHARED_CONFIG_CHECK=1` &ndash; Disable the check for using an IIS Shared Configuration when the shared configuration (*applicationHost.config*) is on the same machine as the IIS installation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1173">*Disponível somente para instaladores do ASP.NET Core 2.2 ou Hosting Bundler posterior.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1173">*Only available for ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later Hosting Bundler installers.*</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1174">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1174">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration>.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1175">Reinicie o sistema ou execute os seguintes comandos em um shell de comando:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1175">Restart the system or execute the following commands in a command shell:</span></span>

   ```console
   net stop was /y
   net start w3svc
   ```
   <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1176">A reinicialização do IIS identifica uma alteração no CAMINHO do sistema, que é uma variável de ambiente, realizada pelo instalador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1176">Restarting IIS picks up a change to the system PATH, which is an environment variable, made by the installer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1177">Não é necessário interromper manualmente os sites individuais no IIS ao instalar o pacote de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1177">It isn't necessary to manually stop individual sites in IIS when installing the Hosting Bundle.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1178">Aplicativos hospedados (sites do IIS) são reiniciados quando o IIS é reiniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1178">Hosted apps (IIS sites) restart when IIS restarts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1179">Os aplicativos são iniciados novamente quando recebem sua primeira solicitação, incluindo a partir do [módulo de inicialização do aplicativo](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1179">Apps start up again when they receive their first request, including from the [Application Initialization Module](#application-initialization-module-and-idle-timeout).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1180">ASP.NET Core adota o comportamento de roll-forward para versões de patch de pacotes de estrutura compartilhados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1180">ASP.NET Core adopts roll-forward behavior for patch releases of shared framework packages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1181">Quando os aplicativos hospedados pelo IIS são reiniciados com o IIS, os aplicativos são carregados com as versões de patch mais recentes de seus pacotes referenciados quando recebem sua primeira solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1181">When apps hosted by IIS restart with IIS, the apps load with the latest patch releases of their referenced packages when they receive their first request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1182">Se o IIS não for reiniciado, os aplicativos serão reiniciados e exibirão o comportamento de roll-forward quando seus processos de trabalho forem reciclados e receberem sua primeira solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1182">If IIS isn't restarted, apps restart and exhibit roll-forward behavior when their worker processes are recycled and they receive their first request.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1183">Para obter informações sobre a Configuração Compartilhada do IIS, consulte [Módulo do ASP.NET Core com a Configuração Compartilhada do IIS](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1183">For information on IIS Shared Configuration, see [ASP.NET Core Module with IIS Shared Configuration](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration).</span></span>

## <a name="install-web-deploy-when-publishing-with-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1184">Instalar a Implantação da Web durante a publicação com o Visual Studio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1184">Install Web Deploy when publishing with Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1185">Ao implantar aplicativos para servidores com [Implantação da Web](/iis/install/installing-publishing-technologies/installing-and-configuring-web-deploy-on-iis-80-or-later), instale a versão mais recente da Implantação da Web no servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1185">When deploying apps to servers with [Web Deploy](/iis/install/installing-publishing-technologies/installing-and-configuring-web-deploy-on-iis-80-or-later), install the latest version of Web Deploy on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1186">Para instalar a Implantação da Web, use o [WebPI (Web Platform Installer)](https://www.microsoft.com/web/downloads/platform.aspx) ou obtenha um instalador diretamente no [Centro de Download da Microsoft](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=43717).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1186">To install Web Deploy, use the [Web Platform Installer (WebPI)](https://www.microsoft.com/web/downloads/platform.aspx) or obtain an installer directly from the [Microsoft Download Center](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=43717).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1187">O método preferencial é usar o WebPI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1187">The preferred method is to use WebPI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1188">O WebPI oferece uma instalação autônoma e uma configuração para provedores de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1188">WebPI offers a standalone setup and a configuration for hosting providers.</span></span>

## <a name="create-the-iis-site"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1189">Criar o site do IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1189">Create the IIS site</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1190">No sistema de hospedagem, crie uma pasta para conter arquivos e pastas publicados do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1190">On the hosting system, create a folder to contain the app's published folders and files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1191">Em uma etapa a seguir, o caminho da pasta é fornecido ao IIS como o caminho físico para o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1191">In a following step, the folder's path is provided to IIS as the physical path to the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1192">Para obter mais informações sobre o layout de arquivo e a pasta de implantação de um aplicativo, confira <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1192">For more information on an app's deployment folder and file layout, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1193">No Gerenciador do IIS, abra o nó do servidor no painel **conexões** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1193">In IIS Manager, open the server's node in the **Connections** panel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1194">Clique com botão direito do mouse na pasta **Sites**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1194">Right-click the **Sites** folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1195">Selecione **Adicionar Site** no menu contextual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1195">Select **Add Website** from the contextual menu.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1196">Forneça um **Nome do site** e defina o **Caminho físico** como a pasta de implantação do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1196">Provide a **Site name** and set the **Physical path** to the app's deployment folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1197">Forneça a configuração de **Associação** e crie o site selecionando **OK**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1197">Provide the **Binding** configuration and create the website by selecting **OK**:</span></span>

   ![Forneça o Nome do site, o caminho físico e o Nome do host na etapa Adicionar Site.](index/_static/add-website-ws2016.png)

   > [!WARNING]
   > <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1199">Associações de curinga de nível superior (`http://*:80/` e `http://+:80`) **não** devem ser usadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1199">Top-level wildcard bindings (`http://*:80/` and `http://+:80`) should **not** be used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1200">Associações de curinga de nível superior podem abrir o aplicativo para vulnerabilidades de segurança.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1200">Top-level wildcard bindings can open up your app to security vulnerabilities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1201">Isso se aplica a curingas fortes e fracos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1201">This applies to both strong and weak wildcards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1202">Use nomes de host explícitos em vez de curingas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1202">Use explicit host names rather than wildcards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1203">Associações de curinga de subdomínio (por exemplo, `*.mysub.com`) não têm esse risco de segurança se você controlar o domínio pai completo (em vez de `*.com`, o qual é vulnerável).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1203">Subdomain wildcard binding (for example, `*.mysub.com`) doesn't have this security risk if you control the entire parent domain (as opposed to `*.com`, which is vulnerable).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1204">Veja [rfc7230 section-5.4](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-5.4) para obter mais informações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1204">See [rfc7230 section-5.4](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-5.4) for more information.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1205">No nó do servidor, selecione **Pools de Aplicativos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1205">Under the server's node, select **Application Pools**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1206">Clique com o botão direito do mouse no pool de aplicativos do site e selecione **Configurações Básicas** no menu contextual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1206">Right-click the site's app pool and select **Basic Settings** from the contextual menu.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1207">Na janela **Editar Pool de Aplicativos**, defina a **versão do CLR do .NET** como **Sem Código Gerenciado**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1207">In the **Edit Application Pool** window, set the **.NET CLR version** to **No Managed Code**:</span></span>

   ![Defina Sem Código Gerenciado para a versão do CLR do .NET.](index/_static/edit-apppool-ws2016.png)

    <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1209">O ASP.NET Core é executado em um processo separado e gerencia o runtime.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1209">ASP.NET Core runs in a separate process and manages the runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1210">O ASP.NET Core não depende do carregamento do CLR de Área de trabalho (CLR do .NET)&mdash;o Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) para o .NET Core é inicializado para hospedar o aplicativo no processo de trabalho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1210">ASP.NET Core doesn't rely on loading the desktop CLR (.NET CLR)&mdash;the Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) for .NET Core is booted to host the app in the worker process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1211">Definir a **versão do CLR do .NET** como **Sem Código Gerenciado** é opcional, porém recomendado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1211">Setting the **.NET CLR version** to **No Managed Code** is optional but recommended.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1212">*ASP.NET Core 2.2 ou posterior*: para uma [implantação autocontida](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) de 64 bits (x64) que usa o [modelo de hospedagem em processo](#in-process-hosting-model), desabilite o pool de aplicativos para processos de 32 bits (x86).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1212">*ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later*: For a 64-bit (x64) [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) that uses the [in-process hosting model](#in-process-hosting-model), disable the app pool for 32-bit (x86) processes.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1213">Na barra lateral **Ações** do Gerenciador do IIS > **Pools de Aplicativos**, selecione **Definir Padrões do Pool de Aplicativos** ou **Configurações Avançadas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1213">In the **Actions** sidebar of IIS Manager > **Application Pools**, select **Set Application Pool Defaults** or **Advanced Settings**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1214">Localize **Habilitar Aplicativos de 32 bits** e defina o valor como `False`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1214">Locate **Enable 32-Bit Applications** and set the value to `False`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1215">Essa configuração não afeta os aplicativos implantados para a [hospedagem fora do processo](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#out-of-process-hosting-model).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1215">This setting doesn't affect apps deployed for [out-of-process hosting](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#out-of-process-hosting-model).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1216">Confirme se a identidade do modelo de processo tem as permissões apropriadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1216">Confirm the process model identity has the proper permissions.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1217">Se a identidade padrão do pool de aplicativos (**modelo** > **Identity** de processo) for alterada de **ApplicationPoolIdentity** para outra identidade, verifique se a nova identidade tem as permissões necessárias para acessar a pasta, o banco de dados e outros recursos necessários do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1217">If the default identity of the app pool (**Process Model** > **Identity**) is changed from **ApplicationPoolIdentity** to another identity, verify that the new identity has the required permissions to access the app's folder, database, and other required resources.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1218">Por exemplo, o pool de aplicativos requer acesso de leitura e gravação às pastas nas quais o aplicativo lê e grava os arquivos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1218">For example, the app pool requires read and write access to folders where the app reads and writes files.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1219">**Configuração de Autenticação do Windows (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1219">**Windows Authentication configuration (Optional)**</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1220">Para saber mais, veja [Configurar a Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1220">For more information, see [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

## <a name="deploy-the-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1221">Implantar o aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1221">Deploy the app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1222">Implante o aplicativo na pasta **caminho físico** do IIS que foi estabelecida na seção [Criar o site do IIS](#create-the-iis-site).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1222">Deploy the app to the IIS **Physical path** folder that was established in the [Create the IIS site](#create-the-iis-site) section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1223">[Implantação da Web](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) é o mecanismo recomendado para implantação, mas existem várias opções para mover o aplicativo da pasta *publicar* do projeto para a pasta de implantação do sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1223">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) is the recommended mechanism for deployment, but several options exist for moving the app from the project's *publish* folder to the hosting system's deployment folder.</span></span>

### <a name="web-deploy-with-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1224">Implantação da Web com o Visual Studio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1224">Web Deploy with Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1225">Consulte o tópico [Perfis de publicação do Visual Studio para implantação de aplicativos ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/visual-studio-publish-profiles#publish-profiles) para saber como criar um perfil de publicação para uso com a Implantação da Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1225">See the [Visual Studio publish profiles for ASP.NET Core app deployment](xref:host-and-deploy/visual-studio-publish-profiles#publish-profiles) topic to learn how to create a publish profile for use with Web Deploy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1226">Se o provedor de hospedagem fornecer um Perfil de Publicação ou o suporte para a criação de um, baixe o perfil e importe-o usando a caixa de diálogo **Publicar** do Visual Studio:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1226">If the hosting provider provides a Publish Profile or support for creating one, download their profile and import it using the Visual Studio **Publish** dialog:</span></span>

![Página de caixa de diálogo Publicar](index/_static/pub-dialog.png)

### <a name="web-deploy-outside-of-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1228">Implantação da Web fora do Visual Studio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1228">Web Deploy outside of Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1229">Também é possível usar a [Implantação da Web](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) fora do Visual Studio na linha de comando.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1229">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) can also be used outside of Visual Studio from the command line.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1230">Para obter mais informações, consulte [Ferramenta de Implantação da Web](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/use-the-web-deployment-tool).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1230">For more information, see [Web Deployment Tool](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/use-the-web-deployment-tool).</span></span>

### <a name="alternatives-to-web-deploy"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1231">Alternativas à Implantação da Web</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1231">Alternatives to Web Deploy</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1232">Use qualquer um dos vários métodos para mover o aplicativo para o sistema host, como cópia manual, [Xcopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/xcopy), [Robocopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/robocopy) ou [PowerShell](/powershell/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1232">Use any of several methods to move the app to the hosting system, such as manual copy, [Xcopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/xcopy), [Robocopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/robocopy), or [PowerShell](/powershell/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1233">Para obter mais informações sobre a implantação do ASP.NET Core no IIS, consulte a seção [Recursos de implantação para administradores do IIS](#deployment-resources-for-iis-administrators).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1233">For more information on ASP.NET Core deployment to IIS, see the [Deployment resources for IIS administrators](#deployment-resources-for-iis-administrators) section.</span></span>

## <a name="browse-the-website"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1234">Procurar no site</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1234">Browse the website</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1235">Depois de implantar o aplicativo no sistema de hospedagem, faça uma solicitação para um dos pontos de extremidade públicos do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1235">After the app is deployed to the hosting system, make a request to one of the app's public endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1236">No exemplo a seguir, o site está associado a um **Nome do Host** IIS de `www.mysite.com` na **Porta** `80`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1236">In the following example, the site is bound to an IIS **Host name** of `www.mysite.com` on **Port** `80`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1237">É feita uma solicitação para `http://www.mysite.com`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1237">A request is made to `http://www.mysite.com`:</span></span>

![O navegador Microsoft Edge carregou a página de inicialização do IIS.](index/_static/browsewebsite.png)

## <a name="locked-deployment-files"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1239">Arquivos de implantação bloqueados</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1239">Locked deployment files</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1240">Os arquivos na pasta de implantação são bloqueados quando o aplicativo está em execução.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1240">Files in the deployment folder are locked when the app is running.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1241">Os arquivos bloqueados não podem ser substituídos durante a implantação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1241">Locked files can't be overwritten during deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1242">Para liberar os arquivos bloqueados em uma implantação, interrompa o pool de aplicativos usando **uma** das abordagens a seguir:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1242">To release locked files in a deployment, stop the app pool using **one** of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1243">Use a Implantação da Web e referencie `Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web` no arquivo do projeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1243">Use Web Deploy and reference `Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web` in the project file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1244">Um arquivo *app_offline.htm* é colocado na raiz do diretório de aplicativo da Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1244">An *app_offline.htm* file is placed at the root of the web app directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1245">Quando o arquivo estiver presente, o módulo do ASP.NET Core apenas desligará o aplicativo e servirá o arquivo *app_offline.htm* durante a implantação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1245">When the file is present, the ASP.NET Core Module gracefully shuts down the app and serves the *app_offline.htm* file during the deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1246">Para obter mais informações, consulte [Referência de configuração do módulo do ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#app_offlinehtm).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1246">For more information, see the [ASP.NET Core Module configuration reference](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#app_offlinehtm).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1247">Manualmente interrompa o pool de aplicativos no Gerenciador do IIS no servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1247">Manually stop the app pool in the IIS Manager on the server.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1248">Use o PowerShell para descartar *App_offline. htm* (requer o PowerShell 5 ou posterior):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1248">Use PowerShell to drop *app_offline.htm* (requires PowerShell 5 or later):</span></span>

  ```powershell
  $pathToApp = 'PATH_TO_APP'

  # Stop the AppPool
  New-Item -Path $pathToApp app_offline.htm

  # Provide script commands here to deploy the app

  # Restart the AppPool
  Remove-Item -Path $pathToApp app_offline.htm

  ```

## <a name="data-protection"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1249">Proteção de dados</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1249">Data protection</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1250">A [pilha Proteção de Dados do ASP.NET Core](xref:security/data-protection/introduction) é usada por vários [middlewares](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) ASP.NET Core, incluindo aqueles usados na autenticação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1250">The [ASP.NET Core Data Protection stack](xref:security/data-protection/introduction) is used by several ASP.NET Core [middlewares](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index), including middleware used in authentication.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1251">Mesmo se as APIs de proteção de dados não forem chamadas pelo código do usuário, a proteção de dados deverá ser configurada com um script de implantação ou no código do usuário para criar um [repositório de chaves](xref:security/data-protection/implementation/key-management) criptográfico persistente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1251">Even if Data Protection APIs aren't called by user code, data protection should be configured with a deployment script or in user code to create a persistent cryptographic [key store](xref:security/data-protection/implementation/key-management).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1252">Se a proteção de dados não estiver configurada, as chaves serão mantidas na memória e descartadas quando o aplicativo for reiniciado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1252">If data protection isn't configured, the keys are held in memory and discarded when the app restarts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1253">Se o token de autenticação for armazenado na memória quando o aplicativo for reiniciado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1253">If the key ring is stored in memory when the app restarts:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1254">Todos os tokens de autenticação baseados em cookies serão invalidados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1254">All cookie-based authentication tokens are invalidated.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1255">Os usuários precisam entrar novamente na próxima solicitação deles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1255">Users are required to sign in again on their next request.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1256">Todos os dados protegidos com o token de autenticação não poderão mais ser descriptografados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1256">Any data protected with the key ring can no longer be decrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1257">Isso pode incluir [tokens CSRF](xref:security/anti-request-forgery#aspnet-core-antiforgery-configuration) e [ASP.NET Core cookies TempData do MVC](xref:fundamentals/app-state#tempdata).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1257">This may include [CSRF tokens](xref:security/anti-request-forgery#aspnet-core-antiforgery-configuration) and [ASP.NET Core MVC TempData cookies](xref:fundamentals/app-state#tempdata).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1258">Para configurar a proteção de dados no IIS para persistir o token de autenticação, use **uma** das seguintes abordagens:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1258">To configure data protection under IIS to persist the key ring, use **one** of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1259">**Criar chaves de registro de proteção de dados**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1259">**Create Data Protection Registry Keys**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1260">As chaves de proteção de dados usadas pelos aplicativos ASP.NET Core são armazenadas no registro externo aos aplicativos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1260">Data protection keys used by ASP.NET Core apps are stored in the registry external to the apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1261">Para persistir as chaves de determinado aplicativo, crie uma chave de registro para o pool de aplicativos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1261">To persist the keys for a given app, create registry keys for the app pool.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1262">Para instalações autônomas do IIS não Web Farm, você pode usar o [script Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1 de Proteção de Dados do PowerShell](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/DataProtection/Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1) para cada pool de aplicativos usado com um aplicativo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1262">For standalone, non-webfarm IIS installations, the [Data Protection Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1 PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/DataProtection/Provision-AutoGenKeys.ps1) can be used for each app pool used with an ASP.NET Core app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1263">Esse script cria uma chave de registro no registro HKLM que é acessível apenas para a conta do processo de trabalho do pool de aplicativos do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1263">This script creates a registry key in the HKLM registry that's accessible only to the worker process account of the app's app pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1264">As chaves são criptografadas em repouso usando a DPAPI com uma chave para todo o computador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1264">Keys are encrypted at rest using DPAPI with a machine-wide key.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1265">Em cenários de web farm, um aplicativo pode ser configurado para usar um caminho UNC para armazenar seu token de autenticação de proteção de dados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1265">In web farm scenarios, an app can be configured to use a UNC path to store its data protection key ring.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1266">Por padrão, as chaves de proteção de dados não são criptografadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1266">By default, the data protection keys aren't encrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1267">Garanta que as permissões de arquivo de o compartilhamento de rede sejam limitadas à conta do Windows na qual o aplicativo é executado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1267">Ensure that the file permissions for the network share are limited to the Windows account the app runs under.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1268">Um certificado X509 pode ser usado para proteger chaves em repouso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1268">An X509 certificate can be used to protect keys at rest.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1269">Considere um mecanismo para permitir aos usuários carregar certificados: coloque os certificados no repositório de certificados confiáveis do usuário e certifique-se de que eles estejam disponíveis em todos os computadores nos quais o aplicativo do usuário é executado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1269">Consider a mechanism to allow users to upload certificates: Place certificates into the user's trusted certificate store and ensure they're available on all machines where the user's app runs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1270">Veja [Configurar a proteção de dados do ASP.NET Core](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview) para obter detalhes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1270">See [Configure ASP.NET Core Data Protection](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview) for details.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1271">**Configurar o pool de aplicativos do IIS para carregar o perfil do usuário**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1271">**Configure the IIS Application Pool to load the user profile**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1272">Essa configuração está na seção **Modelo de processo** nas **Configurações avançadas** do pool de aplicativos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1272">This setting is in the **Process Model** section under the **Advanced Settings** for the app pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1273">Defina **carregar perfil** do usuário `True`como.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1273">Set **Load User Profile** to `True`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1274">Quando definido como `True`, as chaves são armazenadas no diretório do perfil do usuário e protegidas usando DPAPI com uma chave específica para a conta de usuário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1274">When set to `True`, keys are stored in the user profile directory and protected using DPAPI with a key specific to the user account.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1275">As chaves são persistidas para a pasta *%LOCALAPPDATA%/ASP.NET/DataProtection-Keys*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1275">Keys are persisted to the *%LOCALAPPDATA%/ASP.NET/DataProtection-Keys* folder.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1276">O [atributo setProfileEnvironment](/iis/configuration/system.applicationhost/applicationpools/add/processmodel#configuration) do pool de aplicativos também deve ser habilitado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1276">The app pool's [setProfileEnvironment attribute](/iis/configuration/system.applicationhost/applicationpools/add/processmodel#configuration) must also be enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1277">O valor padrão de `setProfileEnvironment` é `true`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1277">The default value of `setProfileEnvironment` is `true`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1278">Em alguns cenários (por exemplo, um SO Windows), `setProfileEnvironment` é definido como `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1278">In some scenarios (for example, Windows OS), `setProfileEnvironment` is set to `false`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1279">Se as chaves não estiverem armazenadas no diretório do perfil do usuário como esperado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1279">If keys aren't stored in the user profile directory as expected:</span></span>

  1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1280">navegue até a pasta *%windir%/system32/inetsrv/config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1280">Navigate to the *%windir%/system32/inetsrv/config* folder.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1281">Abra o arquivo *applicationHost.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1281">Open the *applicationHost.config* file.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1282">Localize o elemento `<system.applicationHost><applicationPools><applicationPoolDefaults><processModel>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1282">Locate the `<system.applicationHost><applicationPools><applicationPoolDefaults><processModel>` element.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1283">Confirme se o atributo `setProfileEnvironment` não está presente, que tem como padrão o valor `true`, ou defina explicitamente o valor do atributo como `true`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1283">Confirm that the `setProfileEnvironment` attribute isn't present, which defaults the value to `true`, or explicitly set the attribute's value to `true`.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1284">**Usar o sistema de arquivos como um repositório de tokens de autenticação**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1284">**Use the file system as a key ring store**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1285">Ajuste o código do aplicativo para [usar o sistema de arquivos como um repositório de tokens de autenticação](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1285">Adjust the app code to [use the file system as a key ring store](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1286">Use um certificado X509 para proteger o token de autenticação e verifique se ele é um certificado confiável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1286">Use an X509 certificate to protect the key ring and ensure the certificate is a trusted certificate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1287">Se o certificado for autoassinado, você deverá colocá-lo no repositório Raiz confiável.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1287">If the certificate is self-signed, place the certificate in the Trusted Root store.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1288">Ao usar o IIS em uma web farm:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1288">When using IIS in a web farm:</span></span>

  * <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1289">Use um compartilhamento de arquivos que pode ser acessado por todos os computadores.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1289">Use a file share that all machines can access.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1290">Implante um certificado X509 em cada computador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1290">Deploy an X509 certificate to each machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1291">Configure a [proteção de dados no código](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1291">Configure [data protection in code](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/overview).</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1292">**Definir uma política para todo o computador para proteção de dados**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1292">**Set a machine-wide policy for data protection**</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1293">O sistema de proteção de dados tem suporte limitado para a configuração da [política de todo o computador](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/machine-wide-policy) padrão para todos os aplicativos que consomem as APIs de proteção de dados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1293">The data protection system has limited support for setting a default [machine-wide policy](xref:security/data-protection/configuration/machine-wide-policy) for all apps that consume the Data Protection APIs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1294">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:security/data-protection/introduction>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1294">For more information, see <xref:security/data-protection/introduction>.</span></span>

## <a name="virtual-directories"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1295">Diretórios virtuais</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1295">Virtual Directories</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1296">[Diretórios virtuais IIS](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#virtual-directories) não são compatíveis com aplicativos ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1296">[IIS Virtual Directories](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#virtual-directories) aren't supported with ASP.NET Core apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1297">Um aplicativo pode ser hospedado como um [subaplicativo](#sub-applications).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1297">An app can be hosted as a [sub-application](#sub-applications).</span></span>

## <a name="sub-applications"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1298">Subaplicativos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1298">Sub-applications</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1299">Um aplicativo ASP.NET Core pode ser hospedado como um [subaplicativo IIS (sub-app)](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#applications).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1299">An ASP.NET Core app can be hosted as an [IIS sub-application (sub-app)](/iis/get-started/planning-your-iis-architecture/understanding-sites-applications-and-virtual-directories-on-iis#applications).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1300">A parte do caminho do subaplicativo se torna parte da URL raiz do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1300">The sub-app's path becomes part of the root app's URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1301">Um subaplicativo não deve incluir o módulo do ASP.NET Core como um manipulador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1301">A sub-app shouldn't include the ASP.NET Core Module as a handler.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1302">Se o módulo for adicionado como um manipulador em um arquivo *Web. config* de um subaplicativo, um *erro de servidor interno 500,19* referenciando o arquivo de configuração com falha será recebido ao tentar procurar o subaplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1302">If the module is added as a handler in a sub-app's *web.config* file, a *500.19 Internal Server Error* referencing the faulty config file is received when attempting to browse the sub-app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1303">O seguinte exemplo mostra um arquivo *web.config* publicado de um subaplicativo ASP.NET Core:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1303">The following example shows a published *web.config* file for an ASP.NET Core sub-app:</span></span>

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<configuration>
  <system.webServer>
    <aspNetCore processPath="dotnet" 
      arguments=".\MyApp.dll" 
      stdoutLogEnabled="false" 
      stdoutLogFile=".\logs\stdout" />
  </system.webServer>
</configuration>
```

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1304">Ao hospedar um subaplicativo não ASP.NET Core abaixo de um aplicativo ASP.NET Core, remova explicitamente o manipulador herdado no arquivo *web.config* do subaplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1304">When hosting a non-ASP.NET Core sub-app underneath an ASP.NET Core app, explicitly remove the inherited handler in the sub-app's *web.config* file:</span></span>

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<configuration>
  <system.webServer>
    <handlers>
      <remove name="aspNetCore" />
    </handlers>
    <aspNetCore processPath="dotnet" 
      arguments=".\MyApp.dll" 
      stdoutLogEnabled="false" 
      stdoutLogFile=".\logs\stdout" />
  </system.webServer>
</configuration>
```

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1305">Links de ativos estáticos dentro do subaplicativo devem usar a notação de sinal de til e barra (`~/`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1305">Static asset links within the sub-app should use tilde-slash (`~/`) notation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1306">A notação de sinal de til e barra aciona um [Auxiliar de Marca](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro) para preceder a base de caminho do subaplicativo ao link relativo renderizado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1306">Tilde-slash notation triggers a [Tag Helper](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro) to prepend the sub-app's pathbase to the rendered relative link.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1307">Para um subaplicativo no `/subapp_path`, uma imagem vinculada com `src="~/image.png"` é renderizada como `src="/subapp_path/image.png"`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1307">For a sub-app at `/subapp_path`, an image linked with `src="~/image.png"` is rendered as `src="/subapp_path/image.png"`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1308">O Middleware de Arquivo Estático do aplicativo raiz não processa a solicitação de arquivo estático.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1308">The root app's Static File Middleware doesn't process the static file request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1309">A solicitação é processada pelo Middleware de Arquivo Estático do subaplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1309">The request is processed by the sub-app's Static File Middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1310">Se um atributo de ativo estático `src` for definido como um caminho absoluto (por exemplo, `src="/image.png"`), o link será renderizado sem a base de caminho do subaplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1310">If a static asset's `src` attribute is set to an absolute path (for example, `src="/image.png"`), the link is rendered without the sub-app's pathbase.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1311">O Middleware de Arquivos Estáticos do aplicativo raiz tenta fornecer o ativo do [webroot](xref:fundamentals/index#web-root) da raiz do aplicativo, que resulta em uma resposta *404 – Não encontrado*, a menos que o ativo estático esteja disponível no aplicativo raiz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1311">The root app's Static File Middleware attempts to serve the asset from the root app's [web root](xref:fundamentals/index#web-root), which results in a *404 - Not Found* response unless the static asset is available from the root app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1312">Para hospedar um aplicativo ASP.NET Core como um subaplicativo em outro aplicativo do ASP.NET Core:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1312">To host an ASP.NET Core app as a sub-app under another ASP.NET Core app:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1313">Estabeleça um pool de aplicativos para o subaplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1313">Establish an app pool for the sub-app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1314">Defina a **versão do CLR do .NET** como **Sem Código Gerenciado** porque o Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) do .NET Core é inicializado para hospedar o aplicativo no processo de trabalho, não no CLR de Área de trabalho (CLR do .NET).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1314">Set the **.NET CLR Version** to **No Managed Code** because the Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) for .NET Core is booted to host the app in the worker process, not the desktop CLR (.NET CLR).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1315">Adicione o site raiz no Gerenciador do IIS com o subaplicativo em uma pasta no site raiz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1315">Add the root site in IIS Manager with the sub-app in a folder under the root site.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1316">Clique com o botão direito do mouse na pasta do subaplicativo no Gerenciador do IIS e selecione **Converter em aplicativo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1316">Right-click the sub-app folder in IIS Manager and select **Convert to Application**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1317">Na caixa de diálogo **Adicionar Aplicativo**, use o botão **Selecionar** no **Pool de Aplicativos** para atribuir o pool de aplicativos que você criou ao subaplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1317">In the **Add Application** dialog, use the **Select** button for the **Application Pool** to assign the app pool that you created for the sub-app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1318">Selecione **OK**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1318">Select **OK**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1319">A atribuição de um pool de aplicativos separado para o subaplicativo é um requisito ao usar o modelo de hospedagem em processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1319">The assignment of a separate app pool to the sub-app is a requirement when using the in-process hosting model.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1320">Para obter mais informações sobre o modelo de hospedagem em processo e como configurar o módulo ASP.NET Core <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>, consulte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1320">For more information on the in-process hosting model and configuring the ASP.NET Core Module, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

## <a name="configuration-of-iis-with-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1321">Configuração do IIS com web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1321">Configuration of IIS with web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1322">A configuração do IIS é influenciada pela seção `<system.webServer>` do *web.config* para cenários do IIS que são funcionais para aplicativos ASP.NET Core com o Módulo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1322">IIS configuration is influenced by the `<system.webServer>` section of *web.config* for IIS scenarios that are functional for ASP.NET Core apps with the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1323">Por exemplo, a configuração do IIS é funcional para a compactação dinâmica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1323">For example, IIS configuration is functional for dynamic compression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1324">Se o IIS for configurado no nível do servidor para usar a compactação dinâmica, o elemento `<urlCompression>` no arquivo *web.config* do aplicativo pode desabilitá-la para um aplicativo do ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1324">If IIS is configured at the server level to use dynamic compression, the `<urlCompression>` element in the app's *web.config* file can disable it for an ASP.NET Core app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1325">Para obter mais informações, consulte estes tópicos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1325">For more information, see the following topics:</span></span>

* [<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1326">Referência de configuração \<para System. webserver></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1326">Configuration reference for \<system.webServer></span></span>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/)
* <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>
* <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1327">Para definir variáveis de ambiente para aplicativos individuais executados em pools de aplicativos isolados (compatível com o IIS 10.0+ ou posterior), veja a seção *comando AppCmd.exe* do tópico [Variáveis de ambiente \<environmentVariables>](/iis/configuration/system.applicationHost/applicationPools/add/environmentVariables/#appcmdexe) na documentação de referência do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1327">To set environment variables for individual apps running in isolated app pools (supported for IIS 10.0 or later), see the *AppCmd.exe command* section of the [Environment Variables \<environmentVariables>](/iis/configuration/system.applicationHost/applicationPools/add/environmentVariables/#appcmdexe) topic in the IIS reference documentation.</span></span>

## <a name="configuration-sections-of-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1328">Seções de configuração de web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1328">Configuration sections of web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1329">As seções de configuração de aplicativos ASP.NET 4.x em *web.config* não são usadas por aplicativos ASP.NET Core para configuração:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1329">Configuration sections of ASP.NET 4.x apps in *web.config* aren't used by ASP.NET Core apps for configuration:</span></span>

* `<system.web>`
* `<appSettings>`
* `<connectionStrings>`
* `<location>`

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1330">Aplicativos ASP.NET Core são configurados para usar outros provedores de configuração.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1330">ASP.NET Core apps are configured using other configuration providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1331">Para obter mais informações, consulte [Configuration](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1331">For more information, see [Configuration](xref:fundamentals/configuration/index).</span></span>

## <a name="application-pools"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1332">Pools de aplicativos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1332">Application Pools</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1333">Ao hospedar vários sites em um servidor, é recomendável isolar os aplicativos uns dos outros, executando cada aplicativo em seu próprio pool de aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1333">When hosting multiple websites on a server, we recommend isolating the apps from each other by running each app in its own app pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1334">A caixa de diálogo **Adicionar Site** do IIS usa como padrão essa configuração.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1334">The IIS **Add Website** dialog defaults to this configuration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1335">Quando um **Nome de site** é fornecido, o texto é transferido automaticamente para a caixa de texto **Pool de aplicativos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1335">When a **Site name** is provided, the text is automatically transferred to the **Application pool** textbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1336">Um novo pool de aplicativos é criado usando o nome do site quando você adicionar o site.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1336">A new app pool is created using the site name when the site is added.</span></span>

## <a name="application-pool-identity"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1337">Pool de aplicativosIdentity</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1337">Application Pool Identity</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1338">Uma conta de identidade do pool de aplicativos permite executar um aplicativo em uma conta exclusiva sem a necessidade de criar e gerenciar domínios ou contas locais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1338">An app pool identity account allows an app to run under a unique account without having to create and manage domains or local accounts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1339">No IIS 8.0 ou posterior, o WAS (Processo de trabalho do administrador) do IIS cria uma conta virtual com o nome do novo pool de aplicativos e executa os processos de trabalho do pool de aplicativos nesta conta por padrão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1339">On IIS 8.0 or later, the IIS Admin Worker Process (WAS) creates a virtual account with the name of the new app pool and runs the app pool's worker processes under this account by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1340">No console de gerenciamento do IIS, em **Configurações avançadas** para o pool de aplicativos, **Identity** Verifique se o está definido para usar **ApplicationPoolIdentity**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1340">In the IIS Management Console under **Advanced Settings** for the app pool, ensure that the **Identity** is set to use **ApplicationPoolIdentity**:</span></span>

![Caixa de diálogo Configurações avançadas do pool de aplicativos](index/_static/apppool-identity.png)

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1342">O processo de gerenciamento do IIS cria um identificador seguro com o nome do pool de aplicativos no Sistema de segurança do Windows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1342">The IIS management process creates a secure identifier with the name of the app pool in the Windows Security System.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1343">Os recursos podem ser protegidos usando essa identidade.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1343">Resources can be secured using this identity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1344">No entanto, essa identidade não é uma conta de usuário real e não será mostrada no Console de Gerenciamento de Usuários do Windows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1344">However, this identity isn't a real user account and doesn't show up in the Windows User Management Console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1345">Se o processo de trabalho do IIS requerer acesso elevado ao aplicativo, modifique a ACL (lista de controle de acesso) do diretório que contém o aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1345">If the IIS worker process requires elevated access to the app, modify the Access Control List (ACL) for the directory containing the app:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1346">Abra o Windows Explorer e navegue para o diretório.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1346">Open Windows Explorer and navigate to the directory.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1347">Clique com o botão direito do mouse no diretório e selecione **Propriedades**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1347">Right-click on the directory and select **Properties**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1348">Na guia **Segurança**, selecione o botão **Editar** e, em seguida, no botão **Adicionar**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1348">Under the **Security** tab, select the **Edit** button and then the **Add** button.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1349">Clique no botão **Locais** e verifique se o sistema está selecionado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1349">Select the **Locations** button and make sure the system is selected.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1350">Insira **IIS AppPool\\<nome_pool_aplicativos>** na área **Inserir os nomes de objeto a serem selecionados**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1350">Enter **IIS AppPool\\<app_pool_name>** in **Enter the object names to select** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1351">Selecione o botão **Verificar Nomes**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1351">Select the **Check Names** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1352">Para o *DefaultAppPool*, verifique os nomes usando **IIS AppPool\DefaultAppPool**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1352">For the *DefaultAppPool* check the names using **IIS AppPool\DefaultAppPool**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1353">Quando o botão **Verificar Nomes** é selecionado, um valor de **DefaultAppPool** é indicado na área de nomes de objeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1353">When the **Check Names** button is selected, a value of **DefaultAppPool** is indicated in the object names area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1354">Não é possível inserir o nome do pool de aplicativos diretamente na área de nomes de objeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1354">It isn't possible to enter the app pool name directly into the object names area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1355">Use o formato **IIS AppPool\\<nome_pool_aplicativos>** ao verificar o nome do objeto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1355">Use the **IIS AppPool\\<app_pool_name>** format when checking for the object name.</span></span>

   ![Selecione a caixa de diálogo de usuários ou grupos para a pasta do aplicativo: o nome do pool de aplicativos "DefaultAppPool" é anexado ao "IIS AppPool\" na área de nomes de objeto antes de selecionar"Verificar Nomes".](index/_static/select-users-or-groups-1.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1357">Selecione **OK**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1357">Select **OK**.</span></span>

   ![Selecione a caixa de diálogo de usuários ou grupos para a pasta do aplicativo: depois de selecionar "Verificar Nomes", o nome do objeto "DefaultAppPool" é mostrado na área de nomes de objeto.](index/_static/select-users-or-groups-2.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1359">As permissões de leitura &amp; execução devem ser concedidas por padrão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1359">Read &amp; execute permissions should be granted by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1360">Forneça permissões adicionais conforme necessário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1360">Provide additional permissions as needed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1361">O acesso também pode ser concedido por meio de um prompt de comando usando a ferramenta **ICACLS**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1361">Access can also be granted at a command prompt using the **ICACLS** tool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1362">Usando o *DefaultAppPool* como exemplo, o comando a seguir é usado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1362">Using the *DefaultAppPool* as an example, the following command is used:</span></span>

```console
ICACLS C:\sites\MyWebApp /grant "IIS AppPool\DefaultAppPool":F
```

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1363">Para saber mais, veja o tópico [icacls](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/icacls).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1363">For more information, see the [icacls](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/icacls) topic.</span></span>

## <a name="http2-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1364">Suporte do HTTP/2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1364">HTTP/2 support</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1365">O [HTTP/2](https://httpwg.org/specs/rfc7540.html) é compatível com implantações fora de processo que cumprem os seguintes requisitos básicos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1365">[HTTP/2](https://httpwg.org/specs/rfc7540.html) is supported for out-of-process deployments that meet the following base requirements:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1366">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 ou posterior; IIS 10 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1366">Windows Server 2016/Windows 10 or later; IIS 10 or later</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1367">Conexões de servidor de borda voltadas para o público usam HTTP/2, mas a conexão de proxy reverso para o [servidor Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) usa HTTP/1.1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1367">Public-facing edge server connections use HTTP/2, but the reverse proxy connection to the [Kestrel server](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel) uses HTTP/1.1.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1368">Estrutura de destino: não se aplica a implantações fora de processo, visto que a conexão HTTP/2 é manipulada inteiramente pelo IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1368">Target framework: Not applicable to out-of-process deployments, since the HTTP/2 connection is handled entirely by IIS.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1369">Conexão TLS 1.2 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1369">TLS 1.2 or later connection</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1370">Se uma conexão HTTP/2 for estabelecida, [HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) relatará `HTTP/1.1`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1370">If an HTTP/2 connection is established, [HttpRequest.Protocol](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.Protocol*) reports `HTTP/1.1`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1371">O HTTP/2 está habilitado por padrão.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1371">HTTP/2 is enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1372">As conexões retornarão para HTTP/1.1 se uma conexão HTTP/2 não for estabelecida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1372">Connections fall back to HTTP/1.1 if an HTTP/2 connection isn't established.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1373">Para obter mais informações sobre a configuração de HTTP/2 com implantações do IIS, consulte [HTTP/2 no IIS](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-10/http2-on-iis).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1373">For more information on HTTP/2 configuration with IIS deployments, see [HTTP/2 on IIS](/iis/get-started/whats-new-in-iis-10/http2-on-iis).</span></span>

## <a name="cors-preflight-requests"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1374">Solicitações de simulação do CORS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1374">CORS preflight requests</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1375">*Esta seção só se aplica a aplicativos ASP.NET Core com o .NET Framework como destino.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1375">*This section only applies to ASP.NET Core apps that target the .NET Framework.*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1376">Para um aplicativo ASP.NET Core com o .NET Framework como destino, as solicitações OPTIONS não são passadas para o aplicativo por padrão no IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1376">For an ASP.NET Core app that targets the .NET Framework, OPTIONS requests aren't passed to the app by default in IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf01d-1377">Para saber como configurar os manipuladores do IIS do aplicativo no *Web. config* para passar solicitações de opções, consulte [habilitar solicitações entre origens no ASP.NET Web API 2: como o CORS funciona](/aspnet/web-api/overview/security/enabling-cross-origin-requests-in-web-api#how-cors-works).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf01d-1377">To learn how to configure the app's IIS handlers in *web.config* to pass OPTIONS requests, see [Enable cross-origin requests in ASP.NET Web API 2: How CORS Works](/aspnet/web-api/overview/security/enabling-cross-origin-requests-in-web-api#how-cors-works).</span></span>
